## 37:1-5 — verses 1-5 (shared commentary)

### Translation

# Tafsir of Surat al-Saffat

[It is] Meccan.

Al-Nasa'i said: Isma'il ibn Mas'ud reported to us, Khalid, that is Ibn al-Harith, narrated to us, from Ibn Abi Dhi'b who said: Ibn Abd al-Rahman reported to me, from Salim ibn Abd Allah, from Abd Allah ibn Umar, may Allah be pleased with both of them, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to command us to shorten [the prayer], yet he would lead us in prayer reciting al-Saffat. Al-Nasa'i alone transmitted this.

In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful

Sufyan al-Thawri said, from al-A'mash, from Abu al-Duha, from Masruq, from Abd Allah ibn Mas'ud, may Allah be pleased with him, that he said: {By those ranged in ranks} refers to the angels; {and those who drive vigorously} refers to the angels; {and those who recite the reminder} refers to the angels.

Ibn Abbas, Masruq, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Ikrimah, Mujahid, al-Suddi, Qatadah, and al-Rabi' ibn Anas said the same.

Qatadah said: The angels are ranks in the heaven.

Muslim said: Abu Bakr ibn Abi Shaybah narrated to us, Muhammad ibn Fudayl narrated to us, from Abu Malik al-Ashja'i, from Rib'i, from Hudhayfah, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "We have been favored over other people in three things: our ranks have been made like the ranks of the angels, the entire earth has been made a place of prostration for us, and its soil has been made a means of purification for us when we do not find water."

Muslim also narrated, as did Abu Dawud, al-Nasa'i, and Ibn Majah, from the hadith of al-A'mash, from al-Musayyab ibn Rafi', from Tamim ibn Tarafah, from Jabir ibn Samurah, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "Will you not form ranks as the angels form ranks before their Lord?" We said, "And how do the angels form ranks before their Lord?" He ﷺ said, "They complete the front ranks first, and they stand close together in the rank."

Al-Suddi and others said: The meaning of His saying {and those who drive vigorously} is that they drive the clouds.

Al-Rabi' ibn Anas said: {and those who drive vigorously} means that which Allah has forbidden in the Qur'an. Malik narrated likewise, from Zayd ibn Aslam.

{and those who recite the reminder}: Al-Suddi said: The angels bring the Book and the Qur'an from Allah to mankind. This verse is like His saying, Most High: {And those [angels] delivering a reminder, as justification or warning} [al-Mursalat: 5, 6].

His saying: {Indeed, your God is truly one} this is the matter being sworn to, that He, Most High, there is no god but He, {Lord of the heavens and the earth and what is between them}, that is, of the creatures, {and Lord of the points of sunrise}, that is, He is the Owner who exercises full disposal over creation, having subjected within it the fixed stars and the moving ones, which appear from the east and set in the west. He confined Himself to mentioning the points of sunrise, leaving out the points of sunset, since the former indicates the latter. He made this explicit in His saying: {But no, I swear by the Lord of the points of sunrise and sunset, indeed We are able} [al-Ma'arij: 40]. And He said in another verse: {Lord of the two sunrises and Lord of the two sunsets} [al-Rahman: 17], meaning in winter and summer, for the sun and the moon.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

تَفْسِيرُ سُورَةِ الصَّافَّاتِ

[وَهِيَ] مَكِّيَّةٌ.

قَالَ النَّسَائِيُّ: أَخْبَرَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ مَسْعُودٍ، حَدَّثَنَا خَالِدُ -يَعْنِي ابْنَ الْحَارِثِ-عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي ذِئْبٍ قَالَ: أخبرني بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، عَنْ سَالِمِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، قَالَ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَأْمُرُنَا بِالتَّخْفِيفِ، وَيَؤُمُّنَا بِالصَّافَّاتِ. تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ النَّسَائِيُّ .

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَنِ الرَّحِيمِ

* *

قَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ أَبِي الضُّحَى، عَنْ مَسْرُوقٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: ﴿وَالصَّافَّاتِ صَفًّا﴾ وَهِيَ: الْمَلَائِكَةُ، ﴿فَالزَّاجِرَاتِ زَجْرًا﴾ وَهِيَ: الْمَلَائِكَةُ، ﴿فَالتَّالِيَاتِ ذِكْرًا﴾ هِيَ: الْمَلَائِكَةُ.

وَكَذَا قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمَسْرُوقٌ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْر، وعِكْرِمة، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، والسُّدِّيّ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَالرَّبِيعُ بْنُ أَنَسٍ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: الْمَلَائِكَةُ صُفُوفٌ فِي السَّمَاءِ.

وَقَالَ مُسْلِمٌ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ أَبِي شَيْبَة، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ فُضَيْل، عَنْ أَبِي مَالِكٍ الْأَشْجَعِيِّ، عَنْ رِبْعِيّ، عَنْ حُذَيْفَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ "فُضِّلنا عَلَى النَّاسِ بِثَلَاثٍ: جُعلت صُفُوفُنَا كَصُفُوفِ الْمَلَائِكَةِ، وَجُعِلَتْ لَنَا الْأَرْضُ كُلُّهَا مَسْجِدًا وجُعلت لَنَا تُربتها طَهُورًا إِذَا لَمْ نَجِدِ الْمَاءَ" .

وَقَدْ رَوَى مُسْلِمٌ أَيْضًا، وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ مِنْ حَدِيثِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنِ المُسَيَّب بْنِ رَافِعٍ، عَنْ تَمِيمِ بْنِ طَرَفة، عَنْ جَابِرِ بْنِ سَمُرَة قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم "ألا تَصُفّون كَمَا تَصُفُّ الْمَلَائِكَةُ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ؟ " قُلْنَا: وَكَيْفَ تَصُفُّ الْمَلَائِكَةُ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ؟ قَالَ ﷺ: "يُتِمون الصُّفُوفَ الْمُتَقَدِّمَةَ ويَتَراصون فِي الصَّفِّ" .

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ وَغَيْرُهُ: مَعْنَى قَوْلِهِ ﴿فَالزَّاجِرَاتِ زَجْرًا﴾ أَنَّهَا تَزْجُرُ السَّحَابَ.

وَقَالَ الرَّبِيعُ بْنُ أَنَسٍ: ﴿فَالزَّاجِرَاتِ زَجْرًا﴾ : مَا زَجَرَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ فِي الْقُرْآنِ. وَكَذَا رَوَى مَالِكٌ، عَنْ زيد بن أسلم.

﴿فَالتَّالِيَاتِ ذِكْرًا﴾ قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: الْمَلَائِكَةُ يَجِيئُونَ بِالْكِتَابِ، وَالْقُرْآنِ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ إِلَى النَّاسِ. وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَالْمُلْقِيَاتِ ذِكْرًا عُذْرًا أَوْ نُذْرًا﴾ [الْمُرْسَلَاتِ:٥، ٦] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ إِلَهَكُمْ لَوَاحِدٌ﴾ هَذَا هُوَ الْمُقْسَمُ عَلَيْهِ، أَنَّهُ تَعَالَى لَا إِلَهَ إلا هو ﴿رَبُّ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ وَمَا بَيْنَهُمَا﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْمَخْلُوقَاتِ، ﴿وَرَبُّ الْمَشَارِقِ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ الْمَالِكُ الْمُتَصَرِّفُ فِي الْخَلْقِ بِتَسْخِيرِهِ بِمَا فِيهِ مِنْ كَوَاكِبَ ثَوَابِتَ، وَسَيَّارَاتٍ تَبْدُو مِنَ الْمَشْرِقِ، وَتَغْرُبُ مِنَ الْمَغْرِبِ. وَاكْتَفَى بِذِكْرِ الْمَشَارِقِ عَنِ الْمَغَارِبِ لِدَلَالَتِهَا عَلَيْهِ. وَقَدْ صَرَّحَ بِذَلِكَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَلا أُقْسِمُ بِرَبِّ الْمَشَارِقِ وَالْمَغَارِبِ إِنَّا لَقَادِرُونَ﴾ [الْمَعَارِجِ:٤٠] . وَقَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿رَبُّ الْمَشْرِقَيْنِ وَرَبُّ الْمَغْرِبَيْنِ﴾ [الرَّحْمَنِ:١٧] يَعْنِي فِي الشِّتَاءِ وَالصَّيْفِ، لِلشَّمْسِ وَالْقَمَرِ.

---

## 37:6-10 — verses 6-10 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs us that He adorned the lowest heaven for those on earth who gaze upon it, {with the adornment of the stars}. It has been read both as a genitive construction and as a substitution, and both carry the same meaning. The moving stars and the fixed ones pierce their light through the transparent body of the heaven, so that it gives light to the people of the earth, just as the Almighty said: {And We have indeed adorned the lowest heaven with lamps and made them missiles for the devils, and We have prepared for them the punishment of the blazing fire} [al-Mulk: 5], and He said: {And We have indeed placed in the heaven great stars and adorned it for those who look, and We have guarded it from every accursed devil, except one who steals a hearing, and he is pursued by a clear flaming star} [al-Hijr: 16-18].

His statement here, {and as a protection}, means: and We protected it, a protection, {from every rebellious devil}, meaning the defiant, insolent one. When he intends to steal a hearing, a piercing flaming star comes to him and burns him. That is why He said: {they cannot listen in to the exalted assembly}, meaning so that they cannot reach the exalted assembly, which is the heavens and the angels within them, when they speak of what God reveals of His legislation and His decree, as has already been explained in the hadiths that we cited regarding the Almighty's saying: {until, when terror is removed from their hearts, they say, "What did your Lord say?" They say, "The truth, and He is the Most High, the Most Great"} [Saba: 23]. That is why He said: {and they are hurled}, meaning they are cast, {from every side}, meaning from every direction from which they seek to approach the heaven, {in expulsion}, meaning a bombardment by which they are driven away, repelled, and prevented from reaching that. {And for them is an enduring punishment}, meaning in the Hereafter there is for them a lasting, painful, continuous punishment, just as He said: {and We have prepared for them the punishment of the blazing fire} [al-Mulk: 5].

His statement: {except one who snatches a snatch}, means except one of the devils who snatches the snatch, which is a word he hears from the heaven and casts it down to the one beneath him, and that one casts it down to the one beneath him, and it may happen that the flaming star catches him before he casts it down, or it may happen that, by God's decree, he casts it down before the flaming star reaches him and burns him, so the other one carries it off to the soothsayer, as was mentioned previously in the hadith. That is why He said: {except one who snatches a snatch, and he is pursued by a piercing flaming star}, meaning a luminous one.

Ibn Jarir said: Abu Kurayb related to us, Waki' related to us, from Isra'il, from Abu Ishaq, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn 'Abbas, who said: The devils had seats in the heaven, and they used to listen in on the revelation. He said: The stars did not used to move, and the devils were not used to being cast at. He said: When they heard the revelation, they would descend to the earth and add nine more words to it. He said: When the Messenger of God ﷺ was sent, whenever a devil sat in his seat a flaming star would come and never miss him until it burned him. He said: They complained of this to Iblis, and he said: This is only due to some matter that has occurred. He said: So he sent out his troops, and they found the Messenger of God ﷺ standing in prayer between the two mountains of Nakhlah, Waki' said: meaning the valley of Nakhlah. He said: They returned to Iblis and informed him, and he said: This is the matter that has occurred.

The hadiths transmitted, along with the reports on this subject, will come later regarding the Almighty's statement informing us of what the jinn said: {And indeed we sought to reach the heaven but found it filled with strong guards and flaming stars. And indeed we used to sit in it in stations to listen, but now whoever listens finds a flaming star lying in wait for him. And indeed we do not know whether evil is intended for those on earth or whether their Lord intends for them a right course} [al-Jinn: 8-10].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ زَيَّنَ السَّمَاءَ الدُّنْيَا لِلنَّاظِرِينَ إِلَيْهَا مِنْ أَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ ﴿بِزِينَةٍ الْكَوَاكِبِ﴾ ، قُرِئَ بِالْإِضَافَةِ وَبِالْبَدَلِ، وَكِلَاهُمَا بِمَعْنًى وَاحِدٍ، فَالْكَوَاكِبُ السَّيَّارَةُ وَالثَّوَابِتُ يَثْقُبُ ضَوْءُهَا جِرْمَ السَّمَاءِ الشَّفَّافَ، فَتُضِيءُ لِأَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى ﴿وَلَقَدْ زَيَّنَّا السَّمَاءَ الدُّنْيَا بِمَصَابِيحَ وَجَعَلْنَاهَا رُجُومًا لِلشَّيَاطِينِ وَأَعْتَدْنَا لَهُمْ عَذَابَ السَّعِيرِ﴾ [الْمُلْكِ:٥] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ جَعَلْنَا فِي السَّمَاءِ بُرُوجًا وَزَيَّنَّاهَا لِلنَّاظِرِينَ وَحَفِظْنَاهَا مِنْ كُلِّ شَيْطَانٍ رَجِيمٍ. إِلا مَنِ اسْتَرَقَ السَّمْعَ فَأَتْبَعَهُ شِهَابٌ مُبِينٌ﴾ [الْحِجْرِ:١٦-١٨] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ هَا هُنَا: ﴿وَحِفْظًا﴾ تَقْدِيرُهُ: وَحَفِظْنَاهَا حِفْظًا، ﴿مِنْ كُلِّ شَيْطَانٍ مَارِدٍ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْمُتَمَرِّدَ الْعَاتِيَ إِذَا أَرَادَ أَنْ يَسْتَرِقَ السَّمْعَ، أَتَاهُ شِهَابٌ ثَاقِبٌ فَأَحْرَقَهُ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿لَا يَسَّمَّعُونَ إِلَى الْمَلإ الأعْلَى﴾ أَيْ: لِئَلَّا يَصِلُوا إِلَى الْمَلَأِ الْأَعْلَى، وَهِيَ السَّمَاوَاتُ وَمِنْ فِيهَا مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ، إِذَا تَكَلَّمُوا بِمَا يُوحِيهِ اللَّهُ مِمَّا يَقُولُهُ مِنْ شَرْعِهِ وَقَدَرِهِ، كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ بَيَانُ ذَلِكَ فِي الْأَحَادِيثِ الَّتِي أَوْرَدْنَاهَا عِنْدَ قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا فُزِّعَ عَنْ قُلُوبِهِمْ قَالُوا مَاذَا قَالَ رَبُّكُمْ قَالُوا الْحَقَّ وَهُوَ الْعَلِيُّ الْكَبِيرُ﴾ [سَبَأٍ:٢٣] وَلِهَذَا قَالَ ﴿وَيُقْذَفُون﴾ أَيْ: يُرْمَوْنَ ﴿مِنْ كُلِّ جَانِبٍ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ كُلِّ جِهَةٍ يَقْصِدُونَ السَّمَاءَ مِنْهَا، ﴿دُحُورًا﴾ أَيْ:رَجْمًا يُدْحَرُونَ بِهِ وَيُزْجَرُونَ، وَيُمْنَعُونَ مِنَ الْوُصُولِ إِلَى ذَلِكَ، ﴿وَلَهُمْ عَذَابٌ وَاصِبٌ﴾ أَيْ:فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ لَهُمْ عَذَابٌ دَائِمٌ مُوجِعٌ مُسْتَمِرٌّ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَأَعْتَدْنَا لَهُمْ عَذَابَ السَّعِيرِ﴾ [الْمُلْكِ:٥] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِلا مَنْ خَطِفَ الْخَطْفَةَ﴾ أَيْ: إِلَّا مَنِ اخْتَطَفَ مِنَ الشَّيَاطِينِ الخطفة، وهي الكلمة يسمعها مِنَ السَّمَاءِ فَيُلْقِيهَا إِلَى الَّذِي تَحْتَهُ، وَيُلْقِيهَا الْآخَرُ إِلَى الَّذِي تَحْتَهُ، فَرُبَّمَا أَدْرَكَهُ الشِّهَابُ قَبْلَ أَنْ يُلْقِيَهَا وَرُبَّمَا أَلْقَاهَا بِقَدَرِ اللَّهِ قَبْلَ أَنْ يَأْتِيَهُ الشِّهَابُ فَيُحْرِقَهُ، فَيَذْهَبُ بِهَا الْآخَرُ إِلَى الْكَاهِنِ، كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿إِلا مَنْ خَطِفَ الْخَطْفَةَ فَأَتْبَعَهُ شِهَابٌ ثَاقِبٌ﴾ أَيْ: مُسْتَنِيرٌ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو كُرَيْب، حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيع، عَنْ إِسْرَائِيلَ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبير، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: كَانَ لِلشَّيَاطِينِ مَقَاعِدُ فِي السَّمَاءِ فَكَانُوا يَسْتَمِعُونَ الْوَحْيَ. قَالَ: وَكَانَتِ النُّجُومُ لَا تَجْرِي، وَكَانَتِ الشَّيَاطِينُ لَا تُرْمى قَالَ: فَإِذَا سَمِعُوا الْوَحْيَ نَزَلُوا إِلَى الْأَرْضِ، فَزَادُوا فِي الْكَلِمَةِ تِسْعًا. قَالَ: فَلَمَّا بُعِثَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، جعل الشَّيْطَانُ إِذَا قَعَدَ مَقْعَدَهُ جَاءَ شِهَابٌ فَلَمْ يُخْطئه حَتَّى يُحرقَه. قَالَ: فَشَكَوْا ذَلِكَ إِلَى إِبْلِيسَ، فَقَالَ: مَا هُوَ إِلَّا مِنْ أمْر حَدَثَ. قَالَ: فَبَثّ جُنُودَهُ، فَإِذَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَائِمٌ يُصَلِّي بَيْنَ جَبَلَيْ نَخْلَةَ -قَالَ وَكِيعٌ: يَعْنِي بَطْنَ نَخْلَةَ-قَالَ: فَرَجَعُوا إِلَى إِبْلِيسَ فَأَخْبَرُوهُ، فَقَالَ: هَذَا الَّذِي حَدَثَ. 

وَسَتَأْتِي الْأَحَادِيثُ الْوَارِدَةُ مَعَ الْآثَارِ فِي هَذَا الْمَعْنَى عِنْدَ قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى إِخْبَارًا عَنِ الْجِنِّ أَنَّهُمْ قَالُوا: ﴿وَأَنَّا لَمَسْنَا السَّمَاءَ فَوَجَدْنَاهَا مُلِئَتْ حَرَسًا شَدِيدًا وَشُهُبًا. وَأَنَّا كُنَّا نَقْعُدُ مِنْهَا مَقَاعِدَ لِلسَّمْعِ فَمَنْ يَسْتَمِعِ الآنَ يَجِدْ لَهُ شِهَابًا رَصَدًا. وَأَنَّا لَا نَدْرِي أَشَرٌّ أُرِيدَ بِمَنْ فِي الأرْضِ أَمْ أَرَادَ بِهِمْ رَبُّهُمْ رَشَدًا﴾ [الْجِنِّ:٨-١٠] .

---

## 37:11-19 — verses 11-19 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: ask these deniers of the resurrection which is harder in creation, they, or the heavens and the earth and what is between them of angels, devils, and mighty creatures? Ibn Mas'ud read it as "Am man 'adadna" (or those We have numbered). They acknowledge that these creations are harder to create than themselves. If that is the case, why do they deny the resurrection, when they witness what is far greater than what they deny? As the Almighty said: {The creation of the heavens and the earth is greater than the creation of mankind, but most people do not know} [Ghafir: 57]. Then He explained that they were created from a weak thing, saying: {Indeed We created them from sticky clay}.

Mujahid, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, and al-Dahhak said: it is the good clay whose parts stick together. Ibn Abbas and Ikrimah said: it is the viscous, sticky clay. Qatadah said: it is that which sticks to the hand.

As for His saying: {Rather you have marveled, while they mock}, meaning: rather you have marveled, O Muhammad, at the disbelief of these deniers of the resurrection, while you are certain and affirming of what Allah has informed of this astonishing matter, namely the restoration of bodies after their annihilation. They, unlike you, out of the intensity of their disbelief, mock what you tell them of this.

Qatadah said: Muhammad ﷺ marveled, while the misguided among the children of Adam mocked. {And when they see a sign}, meaning a clear proof of this, {they ridicule it}. Mujahid and Qatadah said: they mock it.

{And they say, this is nothing but plain magic}, meaning: what you have brought is nothing but plain magic. {When we have died and become dust and bones, shall we indeed be resurrected? Or our forefathers?} They consider that far-fetched and deny it. {Say: Yes, and you will be humbled}, meaning: say to them, O Muhammad: yes, you will be resurrected on the Day of Resurrection after you have become dust and bones, {and you will be humbled}, meaning: made lowly before the tremendous power, as the Almighty said: {And all will come to Him humbled} [al-Naml: 87], and He said: {Indeed those who are arrogant in refusing to worship Me will enter Hell, humbled} [Ghafir: 60].

Then He said: {It will be but a single shout, and behold, they will be looking}, meaning: it is but a single command from Allah, Mighty and Majestic, calling them with a single call to come out of the earth, and behold, they will be standing before Him, looking upon the terrors of the Day of Resurrection.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: فَسَل هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُنْكِرِينَ لِلْبَعْثِ: أَيُّمَا أَشَدُّ خُلُقًا هُمْ أَمِ السَّمَاوَاتُ وَالْأَرْضُ، وَمَا بَيْنَهُمَا مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ وَالشَّيَاطِينِ وَالْمَخْلُوقَاتِ الْعَظِيمَةِ؟ -وَقَرَأَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: "أَمْ مَنْ عَدَدْنَا"-فَإِنَّهُمْ يُقرّون أَنَّ هَذِهِ الْمَخْلُوقَاتِ أَشَدُّ خَلْقًا مِنْهُمْ، وَإِذَا كَانَ الْأَمْرُ كَذَلِكَ فَلِمَ يُنْكِرُونَ الْبَعْثَ؟ وَهُمْ يُشَاهِدُونَ مَا هُوَ أَعْظَمُ مِمَّا أَنْكَرُوا . كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَخَلْقُ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ أَكْبَرُ مِنْ خَلْقِ النَّاسِ وَلَكِنَّ أَكْثَرَ النَّاسِ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ﴾ [غَافِرٍ:٥٧] ثُمَّ بَيَّنَ أَنَّهُمْ خُلقوا مِنْ شَيْءٍ ضَعِيفٍ، فَقَالَ ﴿إِنَّا خَلَقْنَاهُمْ مِنْ طِينٍ لازِبٍ﴾

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ: هُوَ الْجَيِّدُ الَّذِي يَلْتَزِقُ بعضه ببعض. وقال ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ: هُوَ اللَّزِجُ. وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: هُوَ الَّذِي يَلْزَقُ بِالْيَدِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿بَلْ عَجِبْتَ وَيَسْخَرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: بَلْ عَجِبْتَ -يَا مُحَمَّدُ-مِنْ تَكْذِيبِ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُنْكِرِينَ لِلْبَعْثِ، وَأَنْتَ مُوقِنٌ مُصَدِّقٌ بِمَا أَخْبَرَ اللَّهُ بِهِ مِنَ الْأَمْرِ الْعَجِيبِ، وَهُوَ إِعَادَةُ الْأَجْسَامِ بَعْدَ فَنَائِهَا. وَهُمْ بِخِلَافِ أَمْرِكَ، مِنْ شِدَّةِ تَكْذِيبِهِمْ يَسْخَرُونَ مِمَّا تَقُولُ لَهُمْ مِنْ ذَلِكَ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: عَجِبَ مُحَمَّدٌ ﷺ، وسَخِر ضُلال بَنِي آدَمَ. ﴿وَإِذَا رَأَوْا آيَةً﴾ أَيْ: دَلَالَةً وَاضِحَةً عَلَى ذَلِكَ ﴿يَسْتَسْخِرُونَ﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَقَتَادَةُ: يَسْتَهْزِئُونَ.

﴿وَقَالُوا إِنْ هَذَا إِلا سِحْرٌ مُبِينٌ﴾ أَيْ:إِنْ هَذَا الَّذِي جِئْتَ بِهِ إِلَّا سِحْرٌ مُبِينٌ، ﴿أَئِذَا مِتْنَا وَكُنَّا تُرَابًا وَعِظَامًا أَئِنَّا لَمَبْعُوثُونَ، أَوَآبَاؤُنَا الأوَّلُونَ﴾ يَسْتَبْعِدُونَ ذَلِكَ وَيُكَذِّبُونَ بِهِ، ﴿قُلْ نَعَمْ وَأَنْتُمْ دَاخِرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: قُلْ لَهُمْ يَا مُحَمَّدُ: نَعَمْ تُبْعَثُونَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ بَعْدَ مَا تَصِيرُونَ تُرَابًا وَعِظَامًا، ﴿وَأَنْتُمْ دَاخِرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: حَقِيرُونَ تَحْتَ الْقُدْرَةِ الْعَظِيمَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى ﴿وَكُلٌّ أَتَوْهُ دَاخِرِينَ﴾ [النَّمْلِ:٨٧] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ يَسْتَكْبِرُونَ عَنْ عِبَادَتِي سَيَدْخُلُونَ جَهَنَّمَ دَاخِرِينَ﴾ [غَافِرٍ:٦٠] .

ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿فَإِنَّمَا هِيَ زَجْرَةٌ وَاحِدَةٌ فَإِذَا هُمْ يَنْظُرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: إِنما هُوَ أَمْرٌ وَاحِدٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، يَدْعُوهُمْ دَعْوَةً وَاحِدَةً أَنْ يَخْرُجُوا مِنَ الْأَرْضِ، فَإِذَا هُمْ [قِيَامٌ] بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ، يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَى أَهْوَالِ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ.

---

## 37:20-26 — verses 20-26 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty relates the statement of the disbelievers on the Day of Resurrection, that they turn back upon themselves with blame, and acknowledge that they had been wrongdoers to themselves in the worldly abode. When they witness the horrors of the Resurrection, they feel utmost regret, at a point where regret can no longer benefit them. {And they say, "Oh, woe to us! This is the Day of Judgment."} Then the angels and the believers say to them: {This is the Day of Judgment which you used to deny.} This is said to them in a manner of rebuke and reproach. Allah commands the angels to distinguish the disbelievers from the believers at the standing place, in their gathering and resurrection. Therefore the Almighty said: {Gather those who wronged and their spouses (azwajahum)}. Al-Nu'man ibn Bashir, may Allah be pleased with him, said that by "their spouses" is meant those like them and their counterparts. Ibn Abbas, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Ikrimah, Mujahid, al-Suddi, Abu Salih, Abu al-Aliyah, and Zayd ibn Aslam, [and others], said likewise.

Sufyan al-Thawri said, from Simak, from al-Nu'man ibn Bashir, from Umar ibn al-Khattab, may Allah be pleased with him, regarding {Gather those who wronged and their spouses}: he said, their brethren.

Sharik said, from Simak, from al-Nu'man, who said: I heard Umar say regarding {Gather those who wronged and their spouses}: he said, those like them. He said: the practitioner of usury comes together with the practitioners of usury, the practitioner of fornication with the practitioners of fornication, and the practitioner of wine with the practitioners of wine. Khusayf said, from Miqsam, from Ibn Abbas: {their spouses} means their wives. This is gharib (a singular report), and what is well known from him is the first view, as reported by Mujahid and Sa'id ibn Jubayr from him: {their spouses} means their companions.

"And what they used to worship besides Allah," meaning the idols and rivals, will be gathered together with them in their places. His statement: {and guide them to the path of the Blazing Fire} means, direct them to the path of Hell. This is like His statement, the Almighty: {And We will gather them on the Day of Resurrection [fallen] on their faces, blind, dumb, and deaf. Their refuge is Hell; every time it subsides We increase them in blazing fire} [al-Isra: 97].

As for His statement: {And stop them, for they are to be questioned}, meaning: halt them until they are questioned about their deeds and their words which issued from them in the worldly abode, as al-Dahhak said, from Ibn Abbas: meaning, detain them, for they are to be held to account. Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Anas ibn Malik, may Allah be pleased with him, said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whoever calls to something will be held stopped with it until the Day of Resurrection, it will not leave him nor separate from him, even if a man merely called another man." Then he recited: {And stop them, for they are to be questioned}. Al-Tirmidhi related it from the hadith of Layth ibn Abi Sulaym. Ibn Jarir related it from Ya'qub ibn Ibrahim, from Mu'tamir, from Layth, from a man, from Anas, as a marfu' (elevated) report.

Abdullah ibn al-Mubarak said: I heard Uthman ibn Za'idah say: The first thing a man will be questioned about are his companions in sitting. Then it will be said to them, by way of rebuke and reproach: {What is the matter with you, that you do not help one another?}, meaning, as you used to claim that you were altogether victorious and mutually supporting. {Rather, this Day they are in submission}, meaning, submissive to the command of Allah, not opposing it nor deviating from it.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ قِيلِ الْكَفَّارِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ أَنَّهُمْ يَرْجِعُونَ عَلَى أَنْفُسِهِمْ بِالْمَلَامَةِ، وَيَعْتَرِفُونَ بِأَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا ظَالِمِينَ لِأَنْفُسِهِمْ فِي الدَّارِ الدُّنْيَا، فَإِذَا عَايَنُوا أَهْوَالَ الْقِيَامَةِ نَدمُوا كلَّ النَّدَمِ حَيْثُ لَا يَنْفَعُهُمُ النَّدَمُ، ﴿وَقَالُوا يَا وَيْلَنَا هَذَا يَوْمُ الدِّينِ﴾ . فَتَقُولُ لَهُمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ وَالْمُؤْمِنُونَ: ﴿هَذَا يَوْمُ الْفَصْلِ الَّذِي كُنْتُمْ بِهِ تُكَذِّبُونَ﴾ . وَهَذَا يُقَالُ لَهُمْ عَلَى وَجْهِ التَّقْرِيعِ وَالتَّوْبِيخِ، وَيَأْمُرُ اللَّهُ الْمَلَائِكَةَ أَنْ تُميزَ الْكُفَّارَ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ فِي الْمَوْقِفِ فِي مَحْشَرِهِمْ وَمَنْشَرِهِمْ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿احْشُرُوا الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا وَأَزْوَاجَهُمْ﴾ قَالَ النُّعْمَانُ بْنُ بَشِيرٍ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، يَعْنِي بِأَزْوَاجِهِمْ أَشْبَاهَهُمْ وَأَمْثَالَهُمْ. وَكَذَا قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وسعيد بْنُ جُبَيْر، وعِكْرِمة وَمُجَاهِدٌ، والسُّدِّي، وَأَبُو صَالِحٍ، وَأَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ، وَزَيْدُ بْنُ أَسْلَمَ [وَغَيْرُهُمْ] .

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ سمَاك، عَنِ النُّعْمَانِ بْنِ بَشِيرٍ، عَنْ عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ ﴿احْشُرُوا الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا وَأَزْوَاجَهُمْ﴾ قَالَ إِخْوَانَهُمْ: .

وَقَالَ شَرِيكٌ، عَنْ سِمَاكٍ، عَنِ النُّعْمَانِ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ عُمَرَ يَقُولُ ﴿احْشُرُوا الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا وَأَزْوَاجَهُمْ﴾ قَالَ:أَشْبَاهَهُمْ قَالَ: يَجِيءُ صَاحِبُ الرِّبَا مَعَ أَصْحَابِ الرِّبَا، وَصَاحِبُ الزِّنَا مَعَ أَصْحَابِ الزِّنَا، وَصَاحِبُ الْخَمْرِ مَعَ أَصْحَابِ الْخَمْرِ، وَقَالَ خُصَيْف، عَنْ مِقْسَم، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿أَزْوَاجَهُمْ﴾ : نِسَاءَهُمْ. وَهَذَا غَرِيبٌ، وَالْمَعْرُوفُ عَنْهُ الْأَوَّلُ، كَمَا رَوَاهُ مُجَاهِدٌ وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنْهُ: ﴿أَزْوَاجَهُمْ﴾ :قُرَناءهم .

"وَمَا كَانُوا يَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ" أَيْ: مِنَ الْأَصْنَامِ وَالْأَنْدَادِ، تُحْشَرُ مَعَهُمْ فِي أَمَاكِنِهِمْ. وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَاهْدُوهُمْ إِلَى صِرَاطِ الْجَحِيمِ﴾ أَيْ: أَرْشَدُوهُمْ إِلَى طَرِيقِ جَهَنَّمَ، وَهَذَا كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَنَحْشُرُهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ عَلَى وُجُوهِهِمْ عُمْيًا وَبُكْمًا وَصُمًّا مَأْوَاهُمْ جَهَنَّمُ كُلَّمَا خَبَتْ زِدْنَاهُمْ سَعِيرًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ:٩٧] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَقِفُوهُمْ إِنَّهُمْ مَسْئُولُونَ﴾ أَيْ: قِفُوهُمْ حَتَّى يُسألوا عَنْ أَعْمَالِهِمْ وَأَقْوَالِهِمُ الَّتِي صَدَرَتْ عَنْهُمْ فِي الدَّارِ الدُّنْيَا كَمَا قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: يَعْنِي احْبِسُوهُمْ إِنَّهُمْ مُحَاسَبُونَ. وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا النُّفَيلي، حَدَّثَنَا الْمُعْتَمِرُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ لَيْثًا يُحدّث عَنْ بِشْرٍ، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَيُّمَا دَاعٍ دَعَا إِلَى شَيْءٍ كَانَ مَوْقُوفًا مَعَهُ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ، لَا يُغَادِرُهُ وَلَا يُفَارِقُهُ، وَإِنْ دَعَا رَجُلٌ رَجُلًا"، ثُمَّ قَرَأَ: ﴿وَقِفُوهُمْ إِنَّهُمْ مَسْئُولُونَ﴾ . وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ لَيْثِ بْنِ أَبِي سُلَيْمٍ. وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، عَنْ يَعْقُوبَ بْنِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَنْ مُعْتَمِرٍ، عَنْ لَيْثٍ، عَنْ رَجُلٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ مَرْفُوعًا .

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ: سَمِعْتُ عُثْمَانَ بْنَ زَائدَةَ يَقُولُ: إِنَّ أَوَّلَ مَا يُسأل عَنْهُ الرَّجُلُ جُلَسَاؤُهُ، ثُمَّ يُقَالُ لَهُمْ عَلَى سَبِيلِ التَّقْرِيعِ وَالتَّوْبِيخِ: ﴿مَا لَكُمْ لَا تَنَاصَرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: كَمَا زَعَمْتُمْ أَنَّكُمْ جَمِيعٌ مُنْتَصِرٌ، ﴿بَلْ هُمُ الْيَوْمَ مُسْتَسْلِمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: مُنْقَادُونَ لِأَمْرِ اللَّهِ، لَا يُخَالِفُونَهُ وَلَا يَحِيدُونَ عنه.

---

## 37:27-37 — verses 27-37 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, exalted is He, mentions that the disbelievers blame one another in the open spaces of the Day of Resurrection, just as they dispute among themselves in the depths of the Fire. {Then those who were weak will say to those who were arrogant, "Indeed, we were your followers, so will you relieve us of a portion of the Fire?" Those who were arrogant will say, "Indeed, all of us are in it. Indeed, Allah has already judged between the servants."} [Ghafir: 47, 48]. And He said: {And if you could see when the wrongdoers are made to stand before their Lord, throwing back the word to one another. Those who were oppressed will say to those who were arrogant, "If not for you, we would have been believers." Those who were arrogant will say to those who were oppressed, "Did we bar you from guidance after it had come to you? Rather, you were criminals." Those who were oppressed will say to those who were arrogant, "Rather, it was your scheming night and day, when you commanded us to disbelieve in Allah and to set up rivals to Him." And they will confide their regret when they see the punishment. And We will put shackles on the necks of those who disbelieved. Are they rewarded except for what they used to do?} [Saba: 31-33].

Here they say to them: {Indeed, you used to come to us from the right.} Al-Dahhak said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas: they say, "You used to overpower us by the power you had over us, for we were weak and you were strong."

Mujahid said: it means "from the direction of truth," which the disbelievers say to the devils.

Qatadah said: mankind said to the jinn: {Indeed, you used to come to us from the right.} He said: from the direction of good, so you would forbid us from it and delay us from it.

Al-Suddi said: "you used to come to us [from the right]" means from the direction of truth, you made falsehood appear pleasing to us and turned us away from the truth.

Al-Hasan said regarding His statement: {Indeed, you used to come to us from the right}: yes, by Allah, he would come to him at every good thing he intended and turn him away from it.

Ibn Zayd said: its meaning is, "you came between us and the good, and you turned us back from Islam, faith, and doing the good that we were commanded to do."

Yazid al-Rishk said: from the direction of "there is no god but Allah." Khusayf said: they mean from the direction of their right hands (i.e., their oaths of trust). Ikrimah said regarding {Indeed, you used to come to us from the right}: he said, from the direction by which we trusted you.

His statement: {They will say, "Rather, you yourselves were not believers."} The leaders among the jinn and mankind say to their followers: the matter is not as you claim. Rather, your hearts were rejecting of faith, receptive to disbelief and disobedience. {And we had no authority over you} meaning: no proof of the validity of what we called you to. {Rather, you were a transgressing people} meaning: rather, there was transgression and overstepping of the truth within you, and this is why you responded to us and abandoned the truth that the prophets brought you, and they established for you the proofs of the validity of what they brought you, but you opposed them.

{So the word of our Lord has come true upon us. Indeed, we are to taste [the punishment]. So we led you astray; indeed, we were leading [others] astray.} The leaders say to those who were oppressed: the word of Allah has come true upon us, that we are among the wretched who taste the punishment on the Day of Resurrection. {So we led you astray} meaning: we called you to misguidance. {Indeed, we were leading [others] astray} meaning: we called you to what we ourselves were in, and you responded to us. Allah, exalted is He, said: {So indeed, they, that Day, will share in the punishment} meaning: all of them will be in the Fire, each according to his measure. {Indeed, thus do We deal with the criminals. Indeed, they were} meaning, in the worldly abode, {when it was said to them, "There is no god but Allah," were arrogant} meaning: they were too arrogant to say it, as the believers say it.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "I have been commanded to fight the people until they say: there is no god but Allah. Whoever says: there is no god but Allah has thereby protected his property and his life from me, except by right, and his reckoning is with Allah. And Allah revealed in His Book," and he mentioned a people who were arrogant, and said: {Indeed, they were, when it was said to them, "There is no god but Allah," arrogant}.

Ibn Abi Hatim also said: [chain] Abu al-Ala said: the Jews will be brought on the Day of Resurrection and it will be said to them: what did you used to worship? They will say: Allah and Uzayr. It will be said to them: take the side of the left. Then the Christians will be brought and it will be said to them: what did you used to worship? They will say: we worship Allah and the Messiah. It will be said to them: take the side of the left. Then the polytheists will be brought and it will be said to them: "there is no god but Allah," but they will be arrogant. Then it will be said to them: "there is no god but Allah," but they will be arrogant. Then it will be said to them: "there is no god but Allah," but they will be arrogant. Then it will be said to them: take the side of the left, Abu Nadrah said: so they will go off faster than birds. Abu al-Ala said: then the Muslims will be brought and it will be said to them: what did you used to worship? They will say: we used to worship Allah. It will be said to them: would you recognize Him if you saw Him? They will say: yes. It will be said to them: how would you recognize Him when you have not seen Him? They will say: we know that there is no equal to Him. He said: so He, blessed and exalted is He, will make Himself known to them, and Allah will save the believers.

{And they say, "Are we indeed to leave our gods for a mad poet?"} meaning: shall we abandon the worship of our gods and the gods of our forefathers because of the word of this mad poet, meaning the Messenger of Allah ﷺ? Allah, exalted is He, said, denying them and refuting them: {Rather, he has come with the truth} meaning: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ came with the truth in all that Allah's law prescribed for him, of reports and demands, {and confirmed the messengers} meaning: he confirmed them in what they informed of him, of praiseworthy attributes and sound methods, and he informed of Allah in His law, His decree, and His command just as they had informed. {Nothing is said to you except what was already said to the messengers before you} the verse. [Fussilat: 43].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَذْكُرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّ الْكُفَّارَ يَتَلَاوَمُونَ فِي عَرَصَاتِ الْقِيَامَةِ، كَمَا يَتَخَاصَمُونَ فِي دَرَكات النَّارِ، ﴿فَيَقُولُ الضُّعَفَاءُ لِلَّذِينَ اسْتَكْبَرُوا إِنَّا كُنَّا لَكُمْ تَبَعًا فَهَلْ أَنْتُمْ مُغْنُونَ عَنَّا نَصِيبًا مِنَ النَّارِ. قَالَ الَّذِينَ اسْتَكْبَرُوا إِنَّا كُلٌّ فِيهَا إِنَّ اللَّهَ قَدْ حَكَمَ بَيْنَ الْعِبَادِ﴾ [غَافِرٍ:٤٧، ٤٨] . وَقَالَ: ﴿وَلَوْ تَرَى إِذِ الظَّالِمُونَ مَوْقُوفُونَ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ يَرْجِعُ بَعْضُهُمْ إِلَى بَعْضٍ الْقَوْلَ يَقُولُ الَّذِينَ اسْتُضْعِفُوا لِلَّذِينَ اسْتَكْبَرُوا لَوْلا أَنْتُمْ لَكُنَّا مُؤْمِنِينَ. قَالَ الَّذِينَ اسْتَكْبَرُوا لِلَّذِينَ اسْتُضْعِفُوا أَنَحْنُ صَدَدْنَاكُمْ عَنِ الْهُدَى بَعْدَ إِذْ جَاءَكُمْ بَلْ كُنْتُمْ مُجْرِمِينَ. وَقَالَ الَّذِينَ اسْتُضْعِفُوا لِلَّذِينَ اسْتَكْبَرُوا بَلْ مَكْرُ اللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ إِذْ تَأْمُرُونَنَا أَنْ نَكْفُرَ بِاللَّهِ وَنَجْعَلَ لَهُ أَنْدَادًا وَأَسَرُّوا النَّدَامَةَ لَمَّا رَأَوُا الْعَذَابَ وَجَعَلْنَا الأغْلالَ فِي أَعْنَاقِ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا هَلْ يُجْزَوْنَ إِلا مَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [سبأ:٣١-٣٣] . قالوا لهم ههنا: ﴿إِنَّكُمْ كُنْتُمْ تَأْتُونَنَا عَنِ الْيَمِينِ﴾ قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: يَقُولُونَ: كُنْتُمْ تَقْهَرُونَنَا بِالْقُدْرَةِ مِنْكُمْ عَلَيْنَا، لِأَنَّا كُنَّا أَذِلَّاءَ وَكُنْتُمْ أَعِزَّاءَ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: يَعْنِي: عَنِ الْحَقِّ، الْكُفَّارُ تَقُولُهُ لِلشَّيَاطِينِ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: قَالَتِ الْإِنْسُ لِلْجِنِّ: ﴿إِنَّكُمْ كُنْتُمْ تَأْتُونَنَا عَنِ الْيَمِينِ﴾ قَالَ: مِنْ قِبَلِ الْخَيْرِ، فَتَنْهُونَا عَنْهُ وَتُبْطِئُونَا عَنْهُ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ تَأْتُونَنَا [عَنِ الْيَمِينِ] مِنْ قِبَلِ الْحَقِّ، تُزَيِّنُونَ لَنَا الْبَاطِلَ، وَتَصُدُّونَا عَنِ الْحَقِّ.

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنَّكُمْ كُنْتُمْ تَأْتُونَنَا عَنِ الْيَمِينِ﴾ إيْ وَاللَّهِ، يَأْتِيهِ عِنْدَ كُلِّ خَيْرٍ يُرِيدُهُ فَيَصُدُّهُ عَنْهُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ: مَعْنَاهُ تَحُولُونَ بَيْنَنَا وَبَيْنَ الْخَيْرِ، وَرَدَدْتُمُونَا عَنِ الْإِسْلَامِ وَالْإِيمَانِ وَالْعَمَلِ بِالْخَيْرِ الَّذِي أَمَرَنَا بِهِ.

وَقَالَ يَزِيدُ الرشْك: مِنْ قِبَلِ "لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ". وَقَالَ خُصيف: يَعْنُونَ مِنْ قِبَلِ مَيَامِنِهِمْ. وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ ﴿إِنَّكُمْ كُنْتُمْ تَأْتُونَنَا عَنِ الْيَمِينِ﴾ ، قَالَ: مِنْ حَيْثُ نَأْمَنُكُمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿قَالُوا بَلْ لَمْ تَكُونُوا مُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ تَقُولُ الْقَادَةُ مِنَ الْجِنِّ، وَالْإِنْسِ لِلْأَتْبَاعِ: مَا الْأَمْرُ كَمَا تَزْعُمُونَ؟ بَلْ كَانَتْ قُلُوبُكُمْ مُنْكِرَةً لِلْإِيمَانِ، قَابِلَةً لِلْكُفْرِ وَالْعِصْيَانِ، ﴿وَمَا كَانَ لَنَا عَلَيْكُمْ مِنْ سُلْطَانٍ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ حُجَّةٍ عَلَى صِحَّةِ مَا دَعَوْنَاكُمْ إِلَيْهِ، ﴿بَلْ كُنْتُمْ قَوْمًا طَاغِينَ﴾ أَيْ: بَلْ كَانَ فِيكُمْ طُغْيَانٌ وَمُجَاوَزَةٌ لِلْحَقِّ، فَلِهَذَا اسْتَجَبْتُمْ لَنَا وَتَرَكْتُمُ الْحَقَّ الَّذِي جَاءَتْكُمْ بِهِ الْأَنْبِيَاءُ، وَأَقَامُوا لَكُمُ الْحُجَجَ عَلَى صِحَّةِ مَا جَاءُوكُمْ بِهِ، فَخَالَفْتُمُوهُمْ.

﴿فَحَقَّ عَلَيْنَا قَوْلُ رَبِّنَا إِنَّا لَذَائِقُونَ فَأَغْوَيْنَاكُمْ إِنَّا كُنَّا غَاوِينَ﴾ ، يَقُولُ الْكُبَرَاءُ لِلْمُسْتَضْعَفِينَ: حَقَّتْ عَلَيْنَا كَلِمَةُ اللَّهِ : إِنَّا مِنَ الْأَشْقِيَاءِ الذَّائِقِينَ الْعَذَابَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، ﴿فَأَغْوَيْنَاكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: دَعَوْنَاكُمْ إِلَى الضَّلَالَةِ، ﴿إِنَّا كُنَّا غَاوِينَ﴾ أَيْ: دَعَوْنَاكُمْ إِلَى مَا نَحْنُ فِيهِ، فَاسْتَجَبْتُمْ لَنَا، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَإِنَّهُمْ يَوْمَئِذٍ فِي الْعَذَابِ مُشْتَرِكُونَ﴾ أَيِ: الْجَمِيعُ فِي النَّارِ، كُلٌّ بِحَسَبِهِ، ﴿إِنَّا كَذَلِكَ نَفْعَلُ بِالْمُجْرِمِينَ إِنَّهُمْ كَانُوا﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدَّارِ الدُّنْيَا ﴿إِذَا قِيلَ لَهُمْ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا اللَّهُ يَسْتَكْبِرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يَسْتَكْبِرُونَ أَنْ يَقُولُوهَا، كَمَا يَقُولُهَا الْمُؤْمِنُونَ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ ابْنُ أَخِي ابْنِ وَهْب، حَدَّثَنَا عَمِّي، حَدَّثَنَا اللَّيْثُ، عَنِ ابْنِ مُسافر -يَعْنِي عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ خَالِدٍ-عَنِ ابْنِ شِهَابٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ الْمُسَيَّبِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيرة، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أُمِرْتُ أَنْ أُقَاتِلَ النَّاسَ حَتَّى يَقُولُوا: لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، فَمَنْ قَالَ: لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ فَقَدْ عَصَمَ مِنِّي مَالَهُ وَنَفْسَهُ إِلَّا بِحَقِّهِ، وحسابه على الله، وأنزل الله في كتابه -وَذَكَرَ قَوْمًا اسْتَكْبَرُوا-فَقَالَ: ﴿إِنَّهُمْ كَانُوا إِذَا قِيلَ لَهُمْ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا اللَّهُ يَسْتَكْبِرُونَ﴾ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَلَمَةَ مُوسَى بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ، حَدَّثَنَا حمَّاد، عَنْ سَعِيدٍ الجُرَيري، عَنْ أَبِي الْعَلَاءِ قَالَ: يُؤْتَى بِالْيَهُودِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ فَيُقَالُ لَهُمْ: مَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْبُدُونَ؟ فَيَقُولُونَ: اللَّهَ وعُزَيرًا. فَيُقَالُ لَهُمْ: خُذُوا ذَاتَ الشِّمَالِ، ثُمَّ يُؤْتَى بِالنَّصَارَى فَيُقَالُ لَهُمْ: مَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْبُدُونَ؟ فَيَقُولُونَ: نَعْبُدُ اللَّهَ وَالْمَسِيحَ. فَيُقَالُ لَهُمْ: خُذُوا ذَاتَ الشِّمَالِ. ثُمَّ يُؤْتَى بِالْمُشْرِكِينَ فَيُقَالُ لَهُمْ: "لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ"، فَيَسْتَكْبِرُونَ. ثُمَّ يُقَالُ لَهُمْ: "لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ"، فَيَسْتَكْبِرُونَ. ثُمَّ يُقَالُ لَهُمْ: "لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ" فَيَسْتَكْبِرُونَ. فَيُقَالُ لَهُمْ: خُذُوا ذَاتَ الشِّمَالِ -قَالَ أَبُو نَضْرَةَ: فَيَنْطَلِقُونَ أَسْرَعَ مِنَ الطَّيْرِ-قَالَ أَبُو الْعَلَاءِ: ثُمَّ يُؤْتَى بِالْمُسْلِمِينَ فَيُقَالُ لَهُمْ: مَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْبُدُونَ؟ فَيَقُولُونَ: كُنَّا نَعْبُدُ اللَّهَ. فَيُقَالُ لَهُمْ: هَلْ تَعْرِفُونَهُ إِذَا رَأَيْتُمُوهُ؟ فَيَقُولُونَ: نَعَمْ. فَيُقَالُ لَهُمْ: فَكَيْفَ تَعْرِفُونَهُ وَلَمْ تَرَوْهُ؟ قَالُوا: نَعْلَمُ أَنَّهُ لَا عِدْلَ لَهُ. قَالَ: فَيَتَعَرَّفُ لَهُمْ تَبَارَكَ وتعالى، وينجي الله المؤمنين.

﴿وَيَقُولُونَ أَئِنَّا لَتَارِكُو آلِهَتِنَا لِشَاعِرٍ مَجْنُونٍ﴾ أَيْ: أَنْحَنُ نَتْرُكُ عِبَادَةَ آلِهَتِنَا وَآلِهَةِ آبَائِنَا عَنْ قَوْلِ [هَذَا] الشَّاعِرِ الْمَجْنُونِ، يَعْنُونَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ؟! قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى تَكْذِيبًا لَهُمْ، وَرَدًّا عَلَيْهِمْ: ﴿بَلْ جَاءَ بِالْحَقِّ﴾ يَعْنِي رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ جَاءَ بِالْحَقِّ فِي جَمِيعِ شرْعة اللَّهِ لَهُ مِنَ الْإِخْبَارِ وَالطَّلَبِ، ﴿وَصَدَّقَ الْمُرْسَلِينَ﴾ أَيْ: صَدَّقَهُمْ فِيمَا أَخْبَرُوهُ عَنْهُ مِنَ الصِّفَاتِ الْحَمِيدَةِ، وَالْمَنَاهِجِ السَّدِيدَةِ، وَأَخْبَرَ عَنِ اللَّهِ فِي شَرْعِهِ [وَقَدَرِهِ] وَأَمْرِهِ كَمَا أَخْبَرُوا، ﴿مَا يُقَالُ لَكَ إِلا مَا قَدْ قِيلَ لِلرُّسُلِ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ﴾ الْآيَةَ [فُصِّلَتْ:٤٣] .

---

## 37:38-49 — verses 38-49 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, addressing mankind: {Indeed, you are tasters of the painful punishment. And you are not recompensed except for what you used to do}. Then He excluded from this His sincere servants, as the Exalted said: {By the time. Indeed, mankind is in loss. Except those who believe and do righteous deeds} [al-Asr: 1-3].

And He said: {We have certainly created man in the best of stature. Then We return him to the lowest of the low. Except those who believe and do righteous deeds} [al-Tin: 4-6]. And He said: {And there is none of you except he will come to it. This is upon your Lord an inevitability decreed. Then We will save those who feared Allah and leave the wrongdoers within it, on their knees} [Maryam: 71-72]. And He said: {Every soul, for what it has earned, is held in pledge. Except the companions of the right} [al-Muddaththir: 38-39]. For this reason He said here: {Except the sincere servants of Allah}, meaning: they do not taste the painful punishment, nor are they subjected to a rigorous reckoning. Rather, their evil deeds are overlooked, if they have any evil deeds, and they are rewarded for good deeds tenfold, up to seven hundredfold, up to many multiples, up to whatever multiplication Allah the Exalted wills.

Concerning His saying: {For those there is a known provision}, Qatada and al-Suddi said: it means Paradise. Then He explained it by His saying: {Fruits}, meaning: of various kinds, {and they will be honored}, meaning: they will be served, provided for, given ease, and given comfort. {In gardens of bliss, upon couches facing one another}. Mujahid said: none of them will look at the back of another's neck.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from Zayd ibn Abi Awfa, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ came out to us and recited this verse, {upon couches facing one another}, [meaning] some of them look at others.

This is a gharib (singular) hadith.

Concerning His saying: {A cup will be circulated among them from a flowing spring. White, delicious to those who drink it. No headache will there be in it, nor will they be intoxicated from it}, just as He said in another verse: {There will circulate among them immortal youths with vessels, pitchers, and a cup from a flowing spring. No headache will they have therefrom, nor will they be intoxicated} [al-Waqi'a: 17-19]. Allah declared the wine of the Hereafter free from the afflictions found in the wine of this world, namely headache of the head, pain of the stomach (which is the ghawl, harm/malady), and the complete loss of one's mind. So He said here: {A cup will be circulated among them from a flowing spring}, meaning: wine from flowing rivers, whose cutting off or exhaustion they need not fear.

Malik said, from Zayd ibn Aslam: it is a flowing wine, white, meaning: its color is radiant, beautiful, and splendid, unlike the wine of this world in its repulsive, poor appearance, whether reddish, black, yellowish, or turbid, or other qualities that a sound disposition finds repellent.

Concerning His saying, Mighty and Majestic is He: {Delicious to those who drink it}, meaning: its taste is good just as its color is, and the goodness of taste is evidence of the goodness of its scent, unlike the wine of this world in all of these respects.

Concerning His saying: {No headache will there be in it}, meaning: it does not produce in them a ghawl, which is stomach pain, as Mujahid, Qatada, and Ibn Zayd said, unlike the wine of this world which causes colic and the like due to its high water content.

It is also said that what is meant by ghawl here is headache of the head. This was also reported from Ibn Abbas.

Qatada said: it is headache of the head and pain of the stomach. And it was also reported from him, and from al-Suddi: it does not steal away their minds, as the poet said:

"The cup kept stealing us away, taking one after another of us."

Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: there is nothing disagreeable or harmful in it. The correct view is that of Mujahid: that it is stomach pain.

Concerning His saying: {nor will they be intoxicated from it}, Mujahid said: it does not take away their minds. Ibn Abbas, Muhammad ibn Ka'b, al-Hasan, Ata' ibn Abi Muslim al-Khurasani, al-Suddi, and others said likewise.

Al-Dahhak said, from Ibn Abbas: wine has four qualities: intoxication, headache, vomiting, and urination. So Allah mentioned the wine of Paradise and declared it free of these qualities, as He mentioned in Surat al-Saffat.

Concerning His saying: {And with them will be women of restrained glances}, meaning: chaste women who look at none but their husbands. So said Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, Zayd ibn Aslam, Qatada, al-Suddi, and others.

Concerning His saying: {'In}, meaning: with beautiful eyes. It is also said: with large eyes, which comes back to the same meaning, namely wide, beautiful eyes. So He described their eyes with beauty and chastity, like the saying of Zulaykha concerning Yusuf, when she adorned him and brought him out before those women, and they were struck with awe and greatly impressed, thinking him an angel from among the angels due to his beauty and radiant appearance. She said: {That is the one about whom you blamed me. And I certainly sought to seduce him, but he firmly refused} [Yusuf: 32], meaning: he is, along with this beauty, chaste, God fearing, and pure, so she showed them his outward beauty and told them of his inward beauty. And likewise the wide eyed maidens of Paradise: {good and beautiful} [al-Rahman: 70]. For this reason He said: {And with them will be women of restrained glances, wide eyed}.

Concerning His saying: {As if they were sheltered eggs}, He described them with the tenderness of their bodies, in the most beautiful of colors.

Ali ibn Abi Talha said, from Ibn Abbas, may Allah be pleased with him and his father: {As if they were sheltered eggs}, meaning: sheltered pearl.

Here the verse of the poet Abu Dahbal is recited from a poem of his:

"She is radiant like the pearl of a diver, set apart from a hidden jewel."

Al-Hasan said: {As if they were sheltered eggs}, meaning: guarded, untouched by hands.

Al-Suddi said: the egg sheltered in its nest.

Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: {As if they were} sheltered eggs, meaning: the inner part of the egg.

Ata' al-Khurasani said: it is the thin membrane that lies between the outer shell and the inner substance of the egg.

Al-Suddi said: {As if they were sheltered eggs}, meaning: the whiteness of the egg when its shell is removed. Ibn Jarir preferred this, because of His saying "sheltered," saying: the outer shell is touched by the wing of the bird and the nest, and hands can reach it, unlike its interior. And Allah knows best.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] from Umm Salama, may Allah be pleased with her, who said: I said, "O Messenger of Allah, tell me about the saying of Allah: {As if they were sheltered eggs}." He said: "Their delicacy is like the delicacy of the membrane that I saw inside the egg, that which lies next to the shell, which is the ghirqi' (inner egg membrane)."

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from Anas, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "I am the first of people to come forth when they are resurrected, and I am their speaker when they arrive as delegations, and I am their bearer of good tidings when they grieve, and I am their intercessor when they are detained. The banner of praise on that day will be in my hand, and I am the noblest of the children of Adam before my Lord, Mighty and Majestic is He, and this is no boast. A thousand servants will circulate around me, as if they were sheltered eggs, or sheltered pearls."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخَاطِبًا لِلنَّاسِ: ﴿إِنَّكُمْ لَذَائِقُو الْعَذَابِ الألِيمِ. وَمَا تُجْزَوْنَ إِلا مَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْمَلُونَ﴾ ، ثُمَّ اسْتَثْنَى مِنْ ذَلِكَ عِبَادَهُ الْمُخْلَصِينَ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى ﴿وَالْعَصْرِ. إِنَّ الإنْسَانَ لَفِي خُسْرٍ. إِلا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ﴾ [الْعَصْرِ:١-٣] .

وَقَالَ: ﴿لَقَدْ خَلَقْنَا الإنْسَانَ فِي أَحْسَنِ تَقْوِيمٍ. ثُمَّ رَدَدْنَاهُ أَسْفَلَ سَافِلِينَ. إِلا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ﴾ [التِّينِ:٤-٦] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَإِنْ مِنْكُمْ إِلا وَارِدُهَا كَانَ عَلَى رَبِّكَ حَتْمًا مَقْضِيًّا. ثُمَّ نُنَجِّي الَّذِينَ اتَّقَوْا وَنَذَرُ الظَّالِمِينَ فِيهَا جِثِيًّا﴾ [مَرْيَمَ:٧١، ٧٢] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿كُلُّ نَفْسٍ بِمَا كَسَبَتْ رَهِينَةٌ. إِلا أَصْحَابَ الْيَمِينِ﴾ [الْمُدَّثِّرِ:٣٨، ٣٩] وَلِهَذَا قَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿إِلا عِبَادَ اللَّهِ الْمُخْلَصِينَ﴾ أَيْ: لَيْسُوا يَذُوقُونَ الْعَذَابَ الْأَلِيمَ، وَلَا يُنَاقَشُونَ فِي الْحِسَابِ، بَلْ يَتَجَاوَزُ عَنْ سَيِّئَاتِهِمْ، إِنْ كَانَ لَهُمْ سَيِّئَاتٌ، وَيُجْزَوْنَ الْحَسَنَةُ بِعَشْرِ أَمْثَالِهَا إِلَى سَبْعِمِائَةِ ضِعْفٍ إِلَى أَضْعَافٍ كَثِيرَةٍ، إِلَى مَا يَشَاءُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى مِنَ التَّضْعِيفِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ لَهُمْ رِزْقٌ مَعْلُومٌ﴾ قَالَ قَتَادَةُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ: يَعْنِي الْجَنَّةَ. ثُمَّ فَسَّرَهُ بِقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى ﴿فَوَاكِهُ﴾ أَيْ: مُتَنَوِّعَةٌ ﴿وَهُمْ مُكْرَمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يُخْدمون [وَيُرْزَقُونَ] وَيُرَفَّهُونَ وَيُنَعَّمُونَ، ﴿فِي جَنَّاتِ النَّعِيمِ. عَلَى سُرُرٍ مُتَقَابِلِينَ﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: لَا يَنْظُرُ بَعْضُهُمْ فِي قَفَا بَعْضٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ عَبْدَكَ الْقَزْوِينِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا حَسَّانُ بْنُ حَسَّانَ، حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ بِشْرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ مَعِينٍ، حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمَ الْقُرَشِيِّ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ شُرَحْبِيلَ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَبِي أَوْفَى قَالَ: خَرَجَ عَلَيْنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَتَلَا هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ ﴿عَلَى سُرُرٍ مُتَقَابِلِينَ﴾ يَنْظُرُ بَعْضُهُمْ إلى بعض.

حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿يُطَافُ عَلَيْهِمْ بِكَأْسٍ مِنْ مَعِينٍ. بَيْضَاءَ لَذَّةٍ لِلشَّارِبِينَ. لَا فِيهَا غَوْلٌ وَلا هُمْ عَنْهَا يُنزفُونَ﴾ ، كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿يَطُوفُ عَلَيْهِمْ وِلْدَانٌ مُخَلَّدُونَ. بِأَكْوَابٍ وَأَبَارِيقَ وَكَأْسٍ مِنْ مَعِينٍ. لَا يُصَدَّعُونَ عَنْهَا وَلا يُنزفُونَ﴾ [الْوَاقِعَةِ:١٧-١٩] فَنَزَّهَ اللَّهُ خَمْرَ الْآخِرَةِ عَنِ الْآفَاتِ الَّتِي فِي خَمْرِ الدُّنْيَا، مِنْ صُدَاعِ الرَّأْسِ وَوَجَعِ الْبَطْنِ -وَهُوَ الْغَوْلُ-وَذَهَابِهَا بِالْعَقْلِ جُمْلَةً، فَقَالَ تَعَالَى هَاهُنَا: ﴿يُطَافُ عَلَيْهِمْ بِكَأْسٍ مِنْ مَعِينٍ﴾ أَيْ: بِخَمْرٍ مِنْ أَنْهَارٍ جَارِيَةٍ، لَا يَخَافُونَ انْقِطَاعَهَا وَلَا فَرَاغَهَا.

قَالَ مَالِكٌ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: خَمْرٌ جَارِيَةٌ بَيْضَاءُ، أَيْ: لَوْنُهَا مُشْرِقٌ حَسَنٌ بَهِيٌّ لَا كَخَمْرِ الدُّنْيَا فِي مَنْظَرِهَا الْبَشِعِ الرَّدِيءِ، مِنْ حُمْرَةٍ أَوْ سَوَادٍ أَوِ اصْفِرَارٍ أَوْ كُدُورَةٍ، إِلَى غَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِمَّا يُنَفِّرُ الطَّبْعَ السَّلِيمَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿لَذَّةٍ لِلشَّارِبِينَ﴾ أَيْ طَعْمُهَا طَيِّبٌ كَلَوْنِهَا، وَطِيبُ الطَّعْمِ دَلِيلٌ عَلَى طِيبِ الرِّيحِ، بِخِلَافِ خَمْرِ الدُّنْيَا فِي جَمِيعِ ذَلِكَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَا فِيهَا غَوْلٌ﴾ يَعْنِي: لَا تُؤَثِّرُ فِيهِمْ غَوْلًا -وَهُوَ وَجَعُ الْبَطْنِ. قَالَهُ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَابْنُ زَيْدٍ-كَمَا تَفْعَلُهُ خَمْرُ الدُّنْيَا مِنَ القُولَنْج وَنَحْوِهُ، لِكَثْرَةِ مَائِيَّتِهَا.

وَقِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ بِالْغَوْلِ هَاهُنَا: صُدَاعُ الرَّأْسِ. وَرُوِيَ هَكَذَا عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: هُوَ صُدَاعُ الرَّأْسِ، وَوَجَعُ الْبَطْنِ. وَعَنْهُ، وَعَنِ السُّدِّيِّ: لَا تَغْتَالُ عُقُولَهُمْ، كَمَا قَالَ الشَّاعِرُ:

فَمَا زَالَتِ الكأسُ تَغْتَالُنا ... وتَذْهبُ بالأوَّل الأوَّلِ 

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: لَا مَكْرُوهَ فِيهَا وَلَا أَذًى. وَالصَّحِيحُ قَوْلُ مُجَاهِدٍ: إِنَّهُ وَجَعُ الْبَطْنِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا هُمْ عَنْهَا يُنزفُونَ﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: لَا تُذْهِبُ عُقُولَهُمْ، وَكَذَا قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وَعَطَاءُ بْنُ أَبِي مُسْلِمٍ الْخُرَاسَانِيُّ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَغَيْرُهُمْ.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: فِي الْخَمْرِ أَرْبَعُ خِصَالٍ: السُّكْرُ، وَالصُّدَاعُ، وَالْقَيْءُ، وَالْبَوْلُ. فَذَكَرَ اللَّهُ خَمْرَ الْجَنَّةِ فَنَزَّهَهَا عَنْ هَذِهِ الْخِصَالِ، كَمَا ذَكَرَ فِي سُورَةِ "الصَّافَّاتِ" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَعِنْدَهُمْ قَاصِرَاتُ الطَّرْفِ﴾ أَيْ: عَفِيفَاتٌ لَا يَنْظُرْنَ إِلَى غَيْرِ أَزْوَاجِهِنَّ. كَذَا قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَزَيْدُ بْنُ أَسْلَمَ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَغَيْرُهُمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿عِينٌ﴾ أَيْ: حِسَانُ الْأَعْيُنِ. وَقِيلَ: ضِخَامُ الْأَعْيُنِ. هُوَ يَرْجِعُ إِلَى الْأَوَّلِ، وَهِيَ النَّجْلَاءُ الْعَيْنَاءُ، فَوَصَفَ عُيُونَهُنَّ بِالْحُسْنِ وَالْعِفَّةِ، كَقَوْلِ زَلِيخَا فِي يُوسُفَ حِينَ جَمَّلَتْهُ وَأَخْرَجَتْهُ عَلَى تِلْكَ النِّسْوَةِ، فَأَعْظَمْنَهُ وَأَكْبَرْنَهُ، وَظَنَنَّ أَنَّهُ مَلَكٌ مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ لِحُسْنِهِ وَبَهَاءِ مَنْظَرِهِ، قَالَتْ: ﴿فَذَلِكُنَّ الَّذِي لُمْتُنَّنِي فِيهِ وَلَقَدْ رَاوَدْتُهُ عَنْ نَفْسِهِ فَاسْتَعْصَمَ﴾ [يُوسُفَ:٣٢] أَيْ: هُوَ مَعَ هَذَا الْجَمَالِ عَفِيفٌ تَقِيٌّ نَقِيٌّ، [فَأَرَتْهُنَّ جَمَالَهُ الظَّاهِرَ وَأَخْبَرَتْهُنَّ بِجَمَالِهِ الْبَاطِنِ] . وَهَكَذَا الْحُورُ الْعِينُ ﴿خَيْرَاتٌ حِسَانٌ﴾ [الرَّحْمَنِ:٧٠] ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَعِنْدَهُمْ قَاصِرَاتُ الطَّرْفِ عِينٌ﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿كَأَنَّهُنَّ بَيْضٌ مَكْنُونٌ﴾ وَصَفَهُنَّ بِتَرَافَةِ الْأَبْدَانِ بِأَحْسَنِ الْأَلْوَانِ.

قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا: ﴿كَأَنَّهُنَّ بَيْضٌ مَكْنُونٌ﴾ يَقُولُ: اللُّؤْلُؤُ الْمَكْنُونُ.

وَيُنْشَدُ هَاهُنَا بَيْتُ أَبِي دَهْبَلَ الشَّاعِرِ فِي قَصِيدَةٍ لَهُ:

وَهْيَ زَهْرَاء مثْلَ لُؤْلُؤَةِ الْغَوَّ ... اصِ مُيِّزَتْ مِن جَوْهَرٍ مكْنُون 

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ: ﴿كَأَنَّهُنَّ بَيْضٌ مَكْنُونٌ﴾ يَعْنِي: مَحْصُونٌ لَمْ تَمَسَّهُ الْأَيْدِي.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: الْبَيْضُ فِي عُشِّهِ مَكْنُونٌ.

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: ﴿ [كَأَنَّهُنَّ] بَيْضٌ مَكْنُونٌ﴾ ، يَعْنِي: بَطْنَ الْبَيْضِ .

وَقَالَ عَطَاءٌ الْخُرَاسَانِيُّ: هُوَ السِّحَاءُ الَّذِي يَكُونُ بَيْنَ قِشْرَتِهِ الْعُلْيَا وَلِبَابِ الْبَيْضَةِ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: ﴿كَأَنَّهُنَّ بَيْضٌ مَكْنُونٌ﴾ يَقُولُ: بَيَاضُ الْبَيْضِ حِينَ يُنْزَعُ قِشْرُهُ. وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ لِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿مَكْنُونٌ﴾ ، قَالَ: وَالْقِشْرَةُ الْعُلْيَا يَمَسُّهَا جَنَاحُ الطَّيْرِ وَالْعُشُّ، وَتَنَالُهَا الْأَيْدِي بِخِلَافِ دَاخِلِهَا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ وَهْبٍ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْفَرَجِ الصَّدَفِيِّ الدِّمْيَاطِيِّ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ هَاشِمٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي كَرِيمَةَ، عَنْ هِشَامٍ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ، عَنْ أُمِّهِ، عَنْ أُمِّ سَلَمَةَ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، قُلْتُ : يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَخْبِرْنِي عَنْ قَوْلِ اللَّهِ: ﴿كَأَنَّهُنَّ بَيْضٌ مَكْنُونٌ﴾ قَالَ: "رِقَّتُهُنَّ كَرِقَّةِ الْجِلْدَةِ الَّتِي رَأَيْتُهَا فِي دَاخِلِ الْبَيْضَةِ، التي تلي القشر وهي الغِرْقِئ" .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو غَسَّانَ النَّهْدِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ السَّلَامِ بْنُ حَرْبٍ، عَنْ لَيْثٍ، عَنِ الرَّبِيعِ بْنِ أَنَسٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَنَا أَوَّلُ النَّاسِ خُرُوجًا إِذَا بُعِثُوا، وَأَنَا خَطِيبُهُمْ إِذَا وَفَدُوا، وَأَنَا مُبَشِّرُهُمْ إِذَا حَزِنُوا، وَأَنَا شَفِيعُهُمْ إِذَا حُبِسُوا، لِوَاءُ الْحَمْدِ يَوْمَئِذٍ بِيَدِي، وَأَنَا أَكْرَمُ وَلَدِ آدَمَ عَلَى رَبِّي عَزَّ وَجَلَّ وَلَا فَخْرَ، يَطُوفُ عَلِيَّ أَلْفُ خَادِمٍ كَأَنَّهُنَّ الْبَيْضُ الْمَكْنُونُ -أَوِ: اللُّؤْلُؤُ الْمَكْنُونُ" .

---

## 37:50-61 — verses 50-61 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Almighty Allah informs us about the people of Paradise, that they turn to one another asking questions, that is, about their circumstances, how they had been in the world, and what they had endured in it. This occurs in the course of their conversation over their drink, their gathering in companionship and their mutual company in their assemblies, while they sit upon couches, with servants before them coming and going, bringing every great good of foods, drinks, garments, and other things which no eye has seen, no ear has heard, and which have never occurred to the heart of any human being. {A speaker among them said: Indeed I had a companion} Mujahid said: meaning a devil.

Al-Awfi related from Ibn Abbas: he is the polytheist man, who had a companion from among the people of faith in the world.

There is no contradiction between the statement of Mujahid and that of Ibn Abbas, for the devil may be from among the jinn, whispering within the soul, or he may be from among mankind, speaking words that the two ears hear, and both kinds are hostile enemies. Allah the Exalted said: {Some of them inspire others with flowery speech in order to deceive} [al-An'am: 112]. Each of the two whispers, as He the Exalted said: {[Say: I seek refuge in the Lord of mankind, the Sovereign of mankind, the God of mankind] from the evil of the retreating whisperer, who whispers in the breasts of mankind, from among the jinn and mankind} [Surat al-Nas]. Therefore: {A speaker among them said: Indeed I had a companion, who used to say: Are you indeed among those who affirm the truth?} That is: do you affirm the resurrection, the raising up, the reckoning, and the recompense?! Meaning, he says this in a manner of astonishment, denial, treating it as far-fetched, disbelief, and stubborn opposition. {When we have died and become dust and bones, shall we indeed be recompensed?} Mujahid and al-Suddi said: "recompensed" means "held to account." Ibn Abbas and Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi said: "rewarded for our deeds."

Then it says: {He said: Will you look down?} That is, will you look over. The believer says this to his companions and fellow sitters among the people of Paradise. {So he looked down and saw him in the midst of the Blazing Fire} Ibn Abbas, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Khulayd al-'Asri, Qatadah, al-Suddi, Ata al-Khurasani, and others said: meaning in the middle of the Blazing Fire.

Al-Hasan al-Basri said: in the middle of the Blazing Fire, as though he were a burning flame.

Qatadah said: it was mentioned to us that he looked down and saw the skulls of the people boiling. And it was mentioned to us that Ka'b al-Ahbar said: in Paradise there are apertures, and when one of its people wishes to look upon his enemy in the Fire, he looks down through them, and this increases him in gratitude.

{He said: By Allah, you nearly ruined me. And were it not for the favor of my Lord, I would have been among those brought forth} The believer says, addressing the disbeliever: by Allah, you nearly destroyed me, had I obeyed you. {And were it not for the favor of my Lord, I would have been among those brought forth}, that is, were it not for Allah's grace upon me, I would have been like you, in the midst of the Blazing Fire where you are, brought forth with you into the punishment. But He bestowed favor upon me and had mercy on me, and guided me to faith, and directed me to His oneness. {And we would never have been guided if Allah had not guided us} [al-A'raf: 43].

His saying: {Are we then not to die, except our first death, and we will not be punished?} This is the speech of the believer, rejoicing for himself over what Allah has given him of eternal abiding in Paradise and dwelling in the abode of honor, wherein there is no death and no punishment. Therefore he said: {Indeed, this is the great triumph}

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ikrimah said: Ibn Abbas, may Allah be pleased with them both, said regarding the saying of Allah, Blessed and Exalted, to the people of Paradise: {Eat and drink in delight for what you used to do} [al-Tur: 19]. Ibn Abbas, may Allah be pleased with them both, said: His saying, "in delight," means: they will not die therein. At that point they said: {Are we then not to die, except our first death, and we will not be punished?}

Al-Hasan al-Basri said: they knew that every bliss is cut short by death, so they said: {Are we then not to die, except our first death, and we will not be punished?} It was said to them: No. So they said: {Indeed, this is the great triumph}

His saying: {For the like of this let the workers work} Qatadah said: this is the speech of the people of Paradise.

Ibn Jarir said: it is the speech of Allah the Exalted, and its meaning is: for the like of this bliss and this triumph let the workers work in this world, so that they may attain it in the Hereafter.

They have mentioned the story of two men who were partners among the Children of Israel, which falls within the general scope of this noble verse.

Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir said: [chain] Furat ibn Tha'labah al-Bahrani said, regarding His saying: {Indeed I had a companion}: there were two men who were partners, and they had accumulated between them eight thousand dinars. One of them had a trade, and the other had no trade. The one who had a trade said to the other: you have no trade, I see nothing for it but that I part from you and divide our wealth with you. So he divided it with him and parted from him. Then the man bought a house for a thousand dinars that had belonged to a king who had died. He called his companion and showed it to him, saying: how do you see this house? I bought it for a thousand dinars. He said: how fine it is! When he left, the man said: O Allah, my companion bought this house for a thousand dinars, and I ask You for a house among the houses of Paradise. Then he gave a thousand dinars in charity. Then he remained as long as Allah willed him to remain, and then he married a woman for a thousand dinars, and invited his companion and prepared food for him. When he came to him he said: I have married a woman for a thousand dinars. He said: how fine this is! When he left, he said: O my Lord, my companion has married a woman for a thousand dinars, and I ask You for a wife among the wide-eyed maidens (al-hur al-'in). So he gave a thousand dinars in charity. Then he remained as long as Allah willed him to remain, and then he bought two gardens for two thousand dinars. He called him and showed them to him, saying: I have bought these two gardens. He said: how fine this is! When he left, he said: O my Lord, my companion has bought two gardens for two thousand dinars, and I ask You for two gardens in Paradise. So he gave two thousand dinars in charity. Then the angel came to the two of them and took their souls. Then he brought this man who had given charity and admitted him into a house that pleased him, and there was a woman appearing whose beauty illuminated what was beneath her. Then he admitted him into two gardens and something that Allah knows best. At that he said: how similar this is to a man whose affair was such and such. He said: that is him, and this dwelling, the two gardens, and the wife are for you. He said: I had a companion who used to say: are you indeed among those who affirm the truth? It was said to him: he is in the Blazing Fire. He said: will you look down? So he looked down and saw him in the midst of the Blazing Fire. Then he said at that: {By Allah, you nearly ruined me. And were it not for the favor of my Lord, I would have been among those brought forth} the verses.

Ibn Jarir said: this supports the reading of those who read "are you indeed among those who affirm the truth (al-musaddiqin)" with the doubled letter.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Abu Hafs Umar ibn Abd al-Rahman al-Abbar said: I asked Isma'il al-Suddi about this verse: {A speaker among them said: Indeed I had a companion, who used to say: Are you indeed among those who affirm the truth?} He said to me: what reminded you of this? I said: I had just recited it and wished to ask you about it. He said: then remember well. There were two partners among the Children of Israel, one a believer and the other a disbeliever, and they separated with six thousand dinars between them, three thousand dinars each. They remained as long as Allah willed them to remain, then they met, and the disbeliever said to the believer: what have you done with your wealth? Have you invested it in anything? Have you traded with it in anything? The believer said to him: no, and what have you done? He said: I bought with it land, palm trees, fruits, and rivers. The believer said to him: have you indeed done so? He said: yes. The believer went back, and when night came he prayed as long as Allah willed him to pray, and when he finished he took a thousand dinars and placed them before him, then said: O Allah, so-and-so, meaning his disbelieving partner, has bought land, palm trees, fruits, and rivers for a thousand dinars, and tomorrow he will die and leave it behind. O Allah, I buy from You with this thousand dinars land, palm trees, fruits, and rivers in Paradise. Then in the morning he distributed it among the poor. Then they remained as long as Allah willed them to remain, then they met, and the disbeliever said to the believer: what have you done with your wealth, have you invested it in anything, have you traded with it in anything? He said: no, and what have you done? He said: my estate had become burdensome to maintain, so I bought slaves for a thousand dinars, who assist me and work for me in it.

The believer said to him, "Did you really do that?" He said, "Yes." He said: The believer went back, and when night came he prayed as much as God willed him to pray. When he finished, he took a thousand dinars and placed them before him, then said: "O God, so-and-so," meaning his disbelieving partner, "has bought a slave from among the slaves of this world for a thousand dinars, who will die tomorrow and leave him, or the two of them will die and leave each other. O God, I am buying from You with these thousand dinars a slave in Paradise." Then in the morning he distributed the money among the poor.

He said: Then the two remained as long as God willed them to remain, then they met again, and the disbeliever said to the believer, "What did you do with your wealth? Did you invest it in anything? Did you trade with it?" He said, "No. What did you do?" He said, "All my affairs have been settled except one thing: so-and-so's husband died, so I gave her a dowry of a thousand dinars, and she brought it to me along with its equal besides." The believer said to him, "Did you really do that?" He said, "Yes."

The believer went back, and when night came he prayed as much as God willed him to pray. When he finished, he took the remaining thousand dinars, placed them before him, and said: "O God, so-and-so," meaning his disbelieving partner, "has married a wife from among the wives of this world, and he will die tomorrow and leave her, or he will die and she will leave him. O God, with these thousand dinars I ask You for a wide-eyed houri in Paradise." Then in the morning he distributed it among the poor.

He said: The believer was left with nothing. He said: He put on a cotton shirt and a woolen cloak, then took a mattock and put it on his shoulder, working at whatever he could and digging with his strength. He said: A man came to him and said, "O servant of God, will you hire yourself to me by the month, month for month, to look after some animals of mine, feeding them and sweeping their dung?" He said, "Yes." He said: So he hired himself out to him by the month, month for month, to look after his animals.

He said: The owner of the animals used to go out every day to look at his animals, and whenever he saw one of them thin, he would seize its head and strike its neck, then say to him, "Did you steal this one's barley last night?" When the believer saw this hardship, he said, "I will surely go to my disbelieving partner and work his land, so that he feeds me this crust of bread each day and clothes me with these two garments when they wear out."

He said: He set off intending to go to him, and when he reached his door in the evening, there was a palace towering into the sky, with gatekeepers around it. He said to them, "Ask permission for me to see the master of this palace, for if you do so it will please him." They said to him, "Go on, if you are truthful, and sleep in a corner, and when morning comes, present yourself to him."

He said: The believer went and spread half of his cloak beneath him and half over him, then slept. When morning came, he went to his partner and presented himself to him. His disbelieving partner came out riding, and when he saw him he recognized him, so he stopped for him, greeted him, and shook his hand. Then he said to him, "Did you not take from the wealth the same as I took?" He said, "Yes indeed, and this is my state and that is your state." He said, "Tell me, what did you do with your wealth?" He said, "Do not ask me about it." He said, "Then what brought you here?" He said, "I have come to work this land of yours, so that you feed me this crust of bread day by day, and clothe me with these two garments when they wear out."

He said, "No, but I will do for you something better than that. But you will see no good from me until you tell me what you did with your wealth." He said, "I lent it out." He said, "To whom?" He said, "To the Solvent, the Faithful One." He said, "Who is that?" He said, "God, my Lord."

He said: While he was still shaking his hand, he pulled his hand away from his, then said, {Are you indeed one of those who believe? When we have died and become dust and bones, shall we indeed be brought to account?} Al-Suddi said: "Brought to account" means "made to render account." He said: The disbeliever went off and left him.

He said: When the believer saw that he was not turning back to him, he went back and left him. The believer lived out his time in hardship, and the disbeliever lived out his time in ease.

He said: When the Day of Resurrection comes and God admits the believer into Paradise, he passes by and finds land, palm trees, fruits, and rivers, and he says, "To whom does this belong?" It is said, "This is yours." He says, "Glory be to God! Has my deed reached such excellence that I should be rewarded with something like this?!"

He said: Then he passes on and finds slaves whose number cannot be counted, and he says, "To whom do these belong?" It is said, "These are yours." He says, "Glory be to God! Has my deed reached such excellence that I should be rewarded with something like this?!"

He said: Then he passes on and finds a dome of hollowed red ruby, in which is a wide-eyed houri, and he says, "To whom does this belong?" It is said, "This is yours." He says, "Glory be to God! Has my deed reached such excellence that I should be rewarded with something like this?!"

He said: Then the believer remembers his disbelieving partner and says, {Indeed, I had a companion who used to say, "Are you indeed one of those who believe? When we have died and become dust and bones, shall we indeed be brought to account?"} He said: Paradise is elevated, and the Fire is a pit into which one falls.

He said: God shows him his partner in the midst of the Blazing Fire, among the people of the Fire. When the believer sees him, he recognizes him, and says, {By God, you almost brought about my ruin. Had it not been for the favor of my Lord, I would have been among those brought there. Are we not then to die, except our first death, and we will not be punished? Indeed, this is the great triumph. For the like of this let the workers work.} in accordance with the favor bestowed upon him.

He said: The believer then remembers the hardship he went through in this world, and he finds nothing among the hardships he endured in this world harder for him than death.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ أَنَّهُ أَقْبَلَ بَعْضُهُمْ عَلَى بَعْضٍ يَتَسَاءَلُونَ، أَيْ: عَنْ أَحْوَالِهِمْ، وَكَيْفَ كَانُوا فِي الدُّنْيَا، وَمَاذَا كَانُوا يُعَانُونَ فِيهَا؟ وَذَلِكَ مِنْ حَدِيثِهِمْ عَلَى شَرَابِهِمْ، وَاجْتِمَاعِهِمْ فِي تُنَادِمِهِمْ وَعِشْرَتِهِمْ فِي مَجَالِسِهِمْ، وَهُمْ جُلُوسٌ عَلَى السُّرُرِ، وَالْخَدَمِ بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِمْ، يَسْعَوْنَ وَيَجِيئُونَ بِكُلِّ خَيْرٍ عَظِيمٍ، مِنْ مَآكِلَ وَمُشَارِبَ وَمَلَابِسَ، وَغَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِمَّا لَا عَيْنٌ رَأَتْ، وَلَا أُذُنٌ سَمِعَتْ، وَلَا خَطَرَ عَلَى قَلْبِ بَشَرٍ. ﴿قَالَ قَائِلٌ مِنْهُمْ إِنِّي كَانَ لِي قَرِينٌ﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: يَعْنِي شَيْطَانًا.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: هُوَ الرَّجُلُ الْمُشْرِكُ، يَكُونُ لَهُ صَاحِبٌ مِنْ أَهَّلَ الْإِيمَانِ فِي الدُّنْيَا.

وَلَا تَنَافِي بَيْنَ كَلَامِ مُجَاهِدٍ، وَابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ؛ فَإِنَّ الشَّيْطَانَ يَكُونُ مِنَ الْجِنِّ فَيُوَسْوِسُ فِي النَّفْسِ، وَيَكُونُ مِنَ الْإِنْسِ فَيَقُولُ كَلَامًا تَسْمَعُهُ الْأُذُنَانِ، وَكِلَاهُمَا مُتَعَادِيَانِ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿يُوحِي بَعْضُهُمْ إِلَى بَعْضٍ زُخْرُفَ الْقَوْلِ غُرُورًا﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:١١٢] وَكُلٌّ مِنْهُمَا يُوَسْوِسُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿ [قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ النَّاسِ. مَلِكِ النَّاسِ. إِلَهِ النَّاسِ] . مِنْ شَرِّ الْوَسْوَاسِ الْخَنَّاسِ. الَّذِي يُوَسْوِسُ فِي صُدُورِ النَّاسِ. مِنَ الْجِنَّةِ وَالنَّاس﴾ [سُورَةُ النَّاسِ] . وَلِهَذَا ﴿قَالَ قَائِلٌ مِنْهُمْ إِنِّي كَانَ لِي قَرِينٌ. يَقُولُ أَئِنَّكَ لَمِنَ الْمُصَدِّقِينَ﴾ أَيْ: أَأَنْتَ تُصَدِّقُ بِالْبَعْثِ وَالنُّشُورِ وَالْحِسَابِ وَالْجَزَاءِ؟! يَعْنِي: يَقُولُ ذَلِكَ عَلَى وَجْهِ التَّعَجُّبِ وَالتَّكْذِيبِ وَالِاسْتِبْعَادِ، وَالْكُفْرِ وَالْعِنَادِ. ﴿أَئِذَا مِتْنَا وَكُنَّا تُرَابًا وَعِظَامًا أَئِنَّا لَمَدِينُونَ﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ: لَمُحَاسَبُونَ؟ وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، ومحمد بن كعب القرظي: لمجزيون بأعمالنا؟.

قَالَ: ﴿قَالَ هَلْ أَنْتُمْ مُطَّلِعُونَ﴾ أَيْ:مُشْرِفُونَ. يَقُولُ الْمُؤْمِنُ لِأَصْحَابِهِ وَجُلَسَائِهِ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ. ﴿فَاطَّلَعَ فَرَآهُ فِي سَوَاءِ الْجَحِيمِ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَخُلَيْدٌ الْعَصْرِيُّ وَقَتَادَةُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَعَطَاءٌ الْخُرَاسَانِيُّ [وَغَيْرُهُمْ] يَعْنِي فِي وَسَطِ الْجَحِيمِ.

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: فِي وَسَطِ الْجَحِيمِ كَأَنَّهُ شِهَابٌ يَتَّقِدُ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ذُكِرَ لَنَا أَنَّهُ اطَّلَعَ فَرَأَى جَمَاجِمَ الْقَوْمِ تَغْلِي. وَذُكِرَ لَنَا أَنَّ كَعْبَ الْأَحْبَارِ قَالَ: فِي الْجَنَّةِ كُوًى إِذَا أَرَادَ أَحَدٌ مِنْ أَهْلِهَا أَنْ يَنْظُرَ إِلَى عَدُوِّهِ فِي النَّارِ اطَّلَعَ فِيهَا، فَازْدَادَ شُكْرًا.

﴿قَالَ تَاللَّهِ إِنْ كِدْتَ لَتُرْدِينِ﴾ يَقُولُ الْمُؤْمِنَ مُخَاطِبًا لِلْكَافِرِ: وَاللَّهِ إِنْ كِدْتَ لَتُهْلِكُنِي لَوْ أَطَعْتُكَ. ﴿وَلَوْلا نِعْمَةُ رَبِّي لَكُنْتُ مِنَ الْمُحْضَرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: وَلَوْلَا فَضْلُ اللَّهِ عَلَيَّ لَكُنْتُ مِثْلَكَ فِي سَوَاءِ الْجَحِيمِ حَيْثُ أَنْتَ، مُحْضَرٌ مَعَكَ فِي الْعَذَابِ، وَلَكِنَّهُ تَفَضَّلَ [عَلَيَّ] وَرَحِمَنِي فَهَدَانِي لِلْإِيمَانِ، وَأَرْشَدَنِي إِلَى تَوْحِيدِهِ ﴿وَمَا كُنَّا لِنَهْتَدِيَ لَوْلا أَنْ هَدَانَا اللَّهُ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ:٤٣] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَفَمَا نَحْنُ بِمَيِّتِينَ. إِلا مَوْتَتَنَا الأولَى وَمَا نَحْنُ بِمُعَذَّبِينَ﴾ هَذَا مِنْ كَلَامِ الْمُؤْمِنِ مُغْبِطًا نَفْسَهُ بِمَا أَعْطَاهُ اللَّهُ مِنَ الْخُلْدِ فِي الْجَنَّةِ وَالْإِقَامَةِ فِي دَارِ الْكَرَامَةِ، لَا مَوْتَ فِيهَا وَلَا عَذَابَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ هَذَا لَهُوَ الْفَوْزُ الْعَظِيمُ﴾

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الظَّهْرَانِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا حَفْصُ بْنُ عُمَرَ العَدَني، حَدَّثَنَا الْحَكَمُ بْنُ أَبَانٍ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، فِي قَوْلِ اللَّهِ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى لِأَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ: ﴿كُلُوا وَاشْرَبُوا هَنِيئًا بِمَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [الطُّورِ:١٩] ، قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا: قَوْلُهُ: ﴿هَنِيئًا﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَمُوتُونَ فِيهَا. فَعِنْدَهَا قَالُوا: ﴿أَفَمَا نَحْنُ بِمَيِّتِينَ. إِلا مَوْتَتَنَا الأولَى وَمَا نَحْنُ بِمُعَذَّبِينَ﴾

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: عَلِمُوا أَنَّ كُلَّ نَعِيمٍ فَإِنَّ الْمَوْتَ يَقْطَعُهُ، فَقَالُوا: ﴿أَفَمَا نَحْنُ بِمَيِّتِينَ. إِلا مَوْتَتَنَا الأولَى وَمَا نَحْنُ بِمُعَذَّبِينَ﴾ ، قِيلَ [لَهُمْ] : لَا. قَالُوا: ﴿إِنَّ هَذَا لَهُوَ الْفَوْزُ الْعَظِيمُ﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لِمِثْلِ هَذَا فَلْيَعْمَلِ الْعَامِلُونَ﴾ قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: هَذَا مِنْ كَلَامِ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: هُوَ مِنْ كَلَامِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى، وَمَعْنَاهُ: لِمِثْلِ هَذَا النَّعِيمِ وَهَذَا الْفَوْزِ فَلْيَعْمَلِ الْعَامِلُونَ فِي الدُّنْيَا، لِيَصِيرُوا إِلَيْهِ فِي الْآخِرَةِ .

وَقَدْ ذَكَرُوا قِصَّةَ رَجُلَيْنِ كَانَا شَرِيكَيْنِ فِي بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، تَدْخُلُ فِي ضِمْنِ عُمُومِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ.

قَالَ أَبُو جَعْفَرِ بْنِ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي إِسْحَاقُ بْنُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ بْنِ حَبِيبِ بْنِ الشَّهِيدِ، حَدَّثَنَا عَتَّابُ بْنُ بَشِيرٍ، عَنْ خُصَيْفٍ، عَنْ فُرَاتِ بْنِ ثَعْلَبَةَ الْبَهْرَانِيِّ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنِّي كَانَ لِي قَرِينٌ﴾ قال: إن رجلين كانا شَرِيكَيْنِ، فَاجْتَمَعَ لَهُمَا ثَمَانِيَةُ آلَافِ دِينَارٍ، وَكَانَ أَحَدُهُمَا لَهُ حِرْفَةٌ، وَالْآخِرُ لَيْسَ لَهُ حِرْفَةٌ، فَقَالَ الَّذِي لَهُ حِرْفَةٌ لِلْآخَرِ: لَيْسَ عِنْدَكَ حِرْفَةٌ، مَا أَرَانِي إِلَّا مُفَارِقُكَ وَمُقَاسِمُكَ، فَقَاسَمَهُ وَفَارَقَهُ، ثُمَّ إِنَّ الرَّجُلَ اشْتَرَى دَارًا بِأَلْفِ دِينَارٍ كَانَتْ لِمَلِكٍ، مَاتَ، فَدَعَا صَاحِبَهُ فَأَرَاهُ فَقَالَ: كَيْفَ تَرَى هَذِهِ الدَّارَ؟ ابْتَعْتُهَا بِأَلْفِ دِينَارٍ؟ قَالَ: مَا أَحْسَنَهَا! فَلَمَّا خَرَجَ قَالَ: اللَّهُمَّ إِنَّ صَاحِبِي ابْتَاعَ هَذِهِ الدَّارَ بِأَلْفِ دِينَارٍ، وَإِنِّي أَسْأَلُكَ دَارًا مِنْ دُورِ الْجَنَّةِ، فَتَصَدَّقَ بِأَلْفِ دِينَارٍ، ثُمَّ مَكَثَ مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَمْكُثَ، ثُمَّ إِنَّهُ تَزَوَّجَ بِامْرَأَةٍ بِأَلْفِ دِينَارٍ، فَدَعَاهُ وَصَنَعَ لَهُ طَعَامًا. فَلَمَّا أَتَاهُ قَالَ: إِنِّي تَزَوَّجْتُ امْرَأَةً بِأَلْفِ دِينَارٍ. قَالَ: مَا أَحْسَنَ هَذَا! فَلَمَّا انْصَرَفَ قَالَ: يَا رَبِّ، إِنَّ صَاحِبِي تَزَوَّجَ امْرَأَةً بِأَلْفِ دِينَارٍ، وَإِنِّي أَسْأَلُكَ امْرَأَةً مِنَ الْحُورِ الْعِينِ. فَتَصَدَّقُ بِأَلْفِ دِينَارٍ، ثُمَّ إِنَّهُ مَكَثَ مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَمْكُثَ. ثُمَّ اشْتَرَى بُسْتَانَيْنِ بِأَلْفَيْ دِينَارٍ، ثُمَّ دَعَاهُ فَأَرَاهُ فَقَالَ: إِنِّي ابْتَعْتُ هَذَيْنِ الْبُسْتَانَيْنِ. فَقَالَ: مَا أَحْسَنَ هَذَا! فَلَمَّا خَرَجَ قَالَ: يَا رَبِّ، إِنَّ صَاحِبِي قَدِ اشْتَرَى بُسْتَانَيْنِ بِأَلْفَيْ دِينَارٍ، وَأَنَا أَسْأَلُكَ بُسْتَانَيْنِ فِي الْجَنَّةِ. فَتَصَدَّقَ بِأَلْفَيْ دِينَارٍ، ثُمَّ إِنِ الْمَلَكَ أَتَاهُمَا فَتَوَفَّاهُمَا، ثُمَّ انْطَلَقَ بِهَذَا الْمُتَصَدِّقِ، فَأَدْخَلَهُ دَارًا تُعْجِبُهُ، وَإِذَا امْرَأَةٌ تَطْلُعُ يُضِيءُ مَا تَحْتَهَا مِنْ حُسْنِهَا، ثُمَّ أَدْخَلَهُ بُسْتَانَيْنِ وَشَيْئًا اللَّهُ بِهِ عَلِيمٌ، فَقَالَ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ: مَا أَشْبَهَ هَذَا بِرَجُلٍ كَانَ مِنْ أَمْرِهِ كَذَا وَكَذَا. قَالَ: فَإِنَّهُ ذَاكَ، وَلَكَ هَذَا الْمَنْزِلُ وَالْبُسْتَانَانِ وَالْمَرْأَةُ. قَالَ: فَإِنَّهُ كَانَ لِي صَاحِبٌ يَقُولُ: أَئِنَّكَ لَمِنَ الْمُصَدِّقِينَ؟ قِيلَ لَهُ: فَإِنَّهُ فِي الْجَحِيمِ. قَالَ: هَلْ أَنْتُمْ مُطَّلِعُونَ؟ فَاطَّلَعَ فَرَآهُ فِي سَوَاءِ الْجَحِيمِ. فَقَالَ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ: ﴿تَاللَّهِ إِنْ كِدْتَ لَتُرْدِينِ. وَلَوْلا نِعْمَةُ رَبِّي لَكُنْتُ مِنَ الْمُحْضَرِينَ﴾ الْآيَاتِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَهَذَا يُقَوِّي قِرَاءَةَ مَنْ قَرَأَ: "أَئِنَّكَ لَمِنَ المُصَّدّقِينَ" بِالتَّشْدِيدِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ عَرَفَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا عُمَرُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ الْأَبَّارُ أَبُو حَفْصٍ قَالَ: سَأَلْتُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ السُّدِّيَّ عَنْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿قَالَ قَائِلٌ مِنْهُمْ إِنِّي كَانَ لِي قَرِينٌ. يَقُولُ أَئِنَّكَ لَمِنَ الْمُصَدِّقِينَ﴾ ؟ قَالَ: فَقَالَ لِي: مَا ذَكَّرَكَ هَذَا؟ قُلْتُ: قَرَأْتُهُ آنِفًا فَأَحْبَبْتُ أَنْ أَسْأَلَكَ عَنْهُ؟ فَقَالَ: أَمَا فَاحْفَظْ، كَانَ شَرِيكَانِ فِي بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، أَحَدُهُمَا مُؤْمِنٌ وَالْآخَرُ كَافِرٌ، فَافْتَرَقَا عَلَى سِتَّةِ آلَافِ دِينَارٍ، كُلُّ وَاحِدٍ مِنْهُمَا ثَلَاثَةُ آلَافِ دِينَارٍ، فَمَكَثَا مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَمْكُثَا، ثُمَّ الْتَقَيَا فَقَالَ الْكَافِرُ لِلْمُؤْمِنِ: مَا صَنَعْتَ فِي مَالِكَ؟ أَضَرَبْتَ بِهِ شَيْئًا؟ أَتَّجَرْتَ بِهِ فِي شَيْءٍ؟ فَقَالَ لَهُ الْمُؤْمِنُ: لَا فَمَا صَنَعْتَ أَنْتَ؟ فَقَالَ: اشْتَرَيْتُ بِهِ أَرْضًا وَنَخْلًا وَثِمَارًا وَأَنْهَارًا قَالَ: فَقَالَ لَهُ الْمُؤْمِنُ: أَوَ فَعَلْتَ؟ قَالَ: نَعَمْ. فَرَجَعَ الْمُؤْمِنُ حَتَّى إِذَا كَانَ اللَّيْلُ صَلَّى مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يُصَلِّيَ، فَلَمَّا انْصَرَفَ أَخَذَ أَلْفَ دِينَارٍ فَوَضَعَهَا بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: اللهم إن فلانا -يعني شريكه الكافر-اشترى أَرْضًا وَنَخْلًا وَثِمَارًا وَأَنْهَارًا بِأَلْفِ دِينَارٍ، ثُمَّ يَمُوتُ غَدًا وَيَتْرُكُهَا، اللَّهُمَّ إِنِّي اشْتَرَيْتُ مِنْكَ بِهَذِهِ الْأَلْفِ دِينَارٍ أَرْضًا وَنَخْلًا وَثِمَارًا وَأَنْهَارًا فِي الْجَنَّةِ. قَالَ: ثُمَّ أَصْبَحَ فَقَسَمَهَا فِي الْمَسَاكِينِ. قَالَ: ثُمَّ مَكَثَا مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ أن يمكثا، ثم التقيا فقال الكافر لِلْمُؤْمِنِ: مَا صَنَعْتَ فِي مَالِكَ، أَضَرَبْتَ بِهِ فِي شَيْءٍ؟ أَتَّجَرْتَ بِهِ فِي شَيْءٍ؟ قَالَ: لَا فَمَا صَنَعْتَ أَنْتَ. قَالَ: كَانَتْ ضَيْعَتِي قَدِ اشْتَدَّ عَلَيَّ مُؤْنَتُهَا، فَاشْتَرَيْتُ رَقِيقًا بِأَلْفِ دِينَارٍ، يَقُومُونَ بِي فِيهَا،
